	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content"><h2  class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-heading fl-heading-text fl-node-kfhja60qr8g4" data-node="kfhja60qr8g4">
			Engage Coveted Decision Makers At The Office	</h2>
<div  class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-rich-text fl-node-m084rltu6s9b" data-node="m084rltu6s9b">
	<p>Captivate is the largest on-the-go news &amp; entertainment network in North America forging powerful connections between brands and decision makers.</p>
<p>Our network of video-first screens deliver unique access to high-value audiences in captive environments. Advanced targeting, premium video activations and campaign measurement opportunity help brands achieve their goals.</p>
<p>A DOOH industry leader, Captivate offers both direct and programmatic advertising solutions to efficiently target affluent consumers &amp; BDMs with spending power.</p>
<p><strong>Influence the Influential with Captivate.</strong></p>

	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content"><h2  class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-heading fl-heading-text fl-node-ovz83al5e6cj" data-node="ovz83al5e6cj">
			Tracking Success	</h2>
<div  class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-rich-text fl-node-slrpuga3mqen" data-node="slrpuga3mqen">
	<p>At Captivate, we invest in agency and brand success, bringing unrivaled access to high-value audiences in brand-safe environments and contextually relevant advertising at multiple touch points along their daily journey. We offer valuable resources to pinpoint audiences and measure campaign effectiveness.</p>

	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content"><h3  class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-heading fl-heading-text fl-node-rkdmpwcog07t" data-node="rkdmpwcog07t">
			Advanced Audience Targeting & Programmatic	</h3>
<div  class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-rich-text fl-node-1sklpzumard5" data-node="1sklpzumard5">
	<p>Reach your target audience through Captivate’s advanced targeting and programmatic solutions that are proven to pinpoint your optimal audience efficiently. Our dynamic planning tools support your campaign goals, including ABM strategies, niche targets, geography, custom targets and more. We make it easy to activate our programmatic tools through the DSP of your choice.</p>
<p>With Captivate’s solutions, you spend budgets wisely on the most promising audiences and markets for the highest ROI potential.</p>
